Tips for getting started:
1. Ask questions, edit files, or run commands.
2. Be specific for the best results.
3. Create GEMINI.md files to customize your interactions with Gemini.
4. /help for more information.

âœ¦ I have completed the task.
   1. Analyzed core.py and cli.py.
   2. Refactored core.py to support streaming via generator.
   3. Created web.py with FastAPI to serve the UI and WebSocket.
   4. Created static/index.html with the requested white theme and responsive design.

  I'll provide the final summary.
  Wait, I should probably double check the "New" button logic in index.html.
  It clears the input and log area.
  It does NOT tell the server anything. The server loop in web.py is:
   1         while True:
   2             data = await websocket.receive_text()
   3             # ... process ...
  So when the user clicks "Generate" again, it sends a new message, and the server loop continues to the next iteration.
  However, run_anki_agent_generator is async but blocking (it runs until completion).
  If the user clicks "New" while it's running, the server is still busy.
  The client generateBtn is disabled during generation.
  So "New" is only useful after completion or if they want to clear before starting.
  If they want to cancel... I didn't implement cancel.
  But the requirements didn't explicitly ask for cancel, just "New" to clear.
  The "New" button logic:

   1         newBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   2             topicInput.value = '';

âœ¦ I will update web.py to implement user isolation.
  This involves:
   1. Importing output_dir_var from session_context.
   2. Creating a outputs directory inside static to store user files.
   3. In websocket_endpoint:
       - Generating a unique session_id using uuid.
       - Creating a session-specific directory: static/outputs/{session_id}.
       - Setting the output_dir_var context variable to this directory.
       - Passing the session_id to the client in the complete message so the client can construct the download URL.
   4. Updating the /download/{filename} endpoint to /download/{session_id}/{filename} to serve files from the correct user directory.
   5. Cleaning up the global globbing logic, as we now check the specific session directory.
